  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if

End Function

    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

        Return ""
